              <noteGrp>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">
                  <p>6.38.3 to 6.38.8 are in different metre (perhaps Indravajrā) with the same
                    content.</p>
                  <p>6.38.8 has only first hemistich.</p>
                  <p>Missing verses 6.38.30ab.</p>
                  <p>Metre break 6.38.13ab 6.38.17ab 6.38.21cd 6.38.28ab.</p>
                </note>

                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.39: <p>Missing verses 109ab, 110cd, 114cd,
                    115ab, 116cd, 117, 118, 119ab , 121cd, 122, 123ab, 125cd, 130, 131, 132, 133,
                    134ab, 135cd, 136, 137ab, 144ab, 147cd, 148ab, 137cd, 167, 171cd, 172, 173, 174,
                    190, 191, 193cd, 195, 196, 197, 198ab, 200cd, 201ab, 202ab, 204cd, 205, 206,
                    207, 211cd, 216ab, 219, 220, 221, 222, 223, 224, 225, 226, 227, 228, 229ab,
                    218cd, 232cd, 233, 234, 235, 236, 237, 238, 239, 240, 241, 242, 243, 244, 253cd,
                    254cd, 255, 256, 257, , 258, 264, 266ab, 267cd, 268ab, 277, 278, 279, 280ab,
                    281ab, 284cd, 286ab, 295-318, 319cd, 323</p>
                  <p>Additions 124a, 135a, 158a, 160, 201a-201c, 210a-210e, 232a-232b, 254a-254c,
                    273a-273g, 294a-294j, 320a-320b</p>
                  <p>- Chapter begins from verse no 104, folio no. 180r</p>
                  <p>- Verse 134ab is given after 128</p>
                  <p>- There are two folios named 183v. In the first 183v folio, there are 7 verses.
                    Content of these 7 verses (273a to 273g) seems different.</p>
                  <p>- Content of 294a to 294j, match with Cakradatta of Cakrapaṇḍita</p>
                </note>

                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.47L <p>Missing verses: 21ab, 22cd, 23ab,
                    29cd, 30ab, 54ab, 75cd, 76, 79ab</p>
                  <p>Additions: 4ef, 11, 12, 54.1ab, 73.1, 73.2, 73.3</p>
                  <p>Metre Break: 31ab, 80ab</p>
                </note>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.3"> aśvagandhā ja śṛṅgī ca śārivātha <unclear>purnarnnavā</unclear> |
            <caesura/>
             sahavidārī ca tathā kaṣāyaḥ pariṣecane | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.4"> tailam abhyaṅga<cb n="2"/>ne kāyaṃ kuṣṭhe sarjarase tathā |
            <caesura/>
             palaṃ kaṣāyainalade tathā girikadaṃbake | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.5"> vaṭāś ca karṇṇakakubhadhātakī<lb n="4"/>tindūkeṣu ca |
            <caesura/>
             kākolyādau gaṇecāpi pāṇīyaṃ sarpir iṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6ab"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.6cd"> gṛdhrolūkapurīṣāṇi tathā yavaphalā<cb n="2"/>ghṛtaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.7"> saṃdhyayor ubhayoḥ kāryam etad uddhūpanaṃ śiśā |
            <caesura/>
             varuṇāriṣṭakamayaṃ rumakaṃ saindhavaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.8"> dhāraye dyāpi satataṃ vacā putrakajīvake |
            <caesura/>
             śu<cb n="3"/>klāḥ sumanaso lājapayaḥ śālyodanaṃ tathā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.9"> valin nivedya gotīrthe revatyaiprayatātmanā |
            <caesura/>
             saṃgame ca <lb n="5"/> bhiṣak snānaṃ kuryād dhātrīkumārayoḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.10"> nānāvastradharādevī citramālyānulepanā |
            <caesura/>
             calatkuṇḍalinī śyā<cb n="2"/>mā revatīte prasīdatu | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.31.11">yām upāsannisatataṃ devyo vividhabhūṣaṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             lamvākarālāvinatā tathaiva vahuputrikā |
            <caesura/>
             raivatī śuṣkanāsā ca sā ca de<cb n="3"/>vī prasīdatām iti || </l>

            <caesura/>

             pa<cb n="2"/>kve tato nne tu vilaṃghanaṃ syāt sampācanam vāpi virecanam vā | </l>

             pītvā surāṃ salavaṇāṃ mūtra<cb n="2"/>kṛcchrāt pramucyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.33"> pṛthakparṇyādivargañ ca mūlaṃ gokṣurakasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             ardhaprasthena toyasya pacet kṣīrañ caturguṇaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.34"> kṣī<lb n="6"/>rāvaśiṣṭaṃn tatpūtaṃ sarpiṣā saha yojitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pibet kṣīran tatas tan tu mūtrakṛcchraharan naraḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.35"> śakṛt <unclear reason="overwriting">kha</unclear>rasya sampī<cb
              n="1"/>ḍya śakṛd vāpy atha vājinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             rasasya tasya kuḍavaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.36"> mustābhayādevadārumūrvāṇām madhukasya ca |
            <caesura/>
             pibed akṣasamaṃ kalkaṃ mūtradoṣa<cb n="2"/>nivāraṇaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.37"> abhayāmalakākṣāṇāṃ kalkaṃ badarasammitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             sahāmbhasā salavaṇaṃ piben mūtrarujāpahan | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.38"> udu<lb n="7"/>mbarasamaṅ kalkaṃ drākṣāyā jalasaṃyutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pibet paryuṣitaṃ rātrau śītaṃ mūtrarujāpahaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.39"> nidigdhikāyāḥ <cb n="1"/>svarasaṃ pibet kuḍavasaṃmitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaharaṃ kālyam atha vā kṣaudrasaṃyutaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.40"> prapīḍyāmalakānāṃ tu rasaṃ kuḍavasaṃmmitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pītvāgadībhavej jantur mū<cb n="2"/>tradoṣarujāturuḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.41"> dhātrīphalarasenaiva sūkṣmelām vā piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasyālābhe suśītena svetataṇḍulavāri<lb n="8"/>ṇā | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.42"> tālasya taruṇam m<unclear reason="faded">ū</unclear>laṃ trapusasya
            rasaṃ tathā |
            <caesura/>
             svetakarkaṭakaś caiva prātas tu payasā pibet | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.43"> srita<cb n="1"/>m vā madhuraiḥ kṣīraṃ sarpirmiśram piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaviśudhyarthaṃ śukradoṣaharaṃ śivaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.44"> balāśvadaṃṣṭrāṃ krauñcāsthikokilākṣakataṇḍulāṃ | <g
              ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/>
            <g ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/>
            <caesura/>
            <pb n="201r" facs="201r IMG_0060.JPG"/><lb n="1"/>śataparvakamūlañ ca devadāru
            sacitraṃkaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.45"> akṣabījañ ca surayā kalkīkṛtya piben naraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mūtradoṣaviśuddhyarthaṃ ta<cb n="1"/>thai<add place="above"><unclear reason="faded"
                >vā</unclear></add>śmaribhedanaṃ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.58.46"> pāṭalākṣaram āhṛtya saptakṛtvaḥ parisrutaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pibet mūtravikāraghnaṃ saṃsṛṣṭan tailamātrayeti || ❈ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.1"> athāto mūtrāghātapratiṣedhaṃ
              <expan>vyā<ex>vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</ex></expan> || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.2"> yadā mūtrayato jantoḥ mūtravego vihanyate |
            <caesura/>
             mūtrāghātaṃ vadanty etam aṣṭa<lb n="2"/>dhā sa tu vakṣyate | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.3"> vātena pittena kaphena sarvais tathābhighātaiḥ śakṛdaśmaribhyāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             tathāparaḥ śarkarayā suka<cb n="1"/>ṣṭo mūtropaghātaḥ paṭhito ṣṭamas tu<del
              rend="crossed out">ḥ</del> | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.4"> alpam alpaṃ bhṛśaṃpīḍya muṣkamehanabastibhiḥ
            <caesura/>
             saṃtudyamānaḥ kṛcchreṇa vātāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.5"> pītam vāpy a<cb n="2"/>tha vā raktaṃ muṣkamehanabastibhir
            <caesura/>
             agnineva ca dahṛmbhiḥ pittāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.6"> samunnaddhodaraḥ kṛcchrān muṣkamehana<lb n="3"/>bastibhiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saṃhṛṣṭaromā gurubhiḥ śleṣmāghātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.7"> dāhaśītarujāviṣṭo nānāvarṇṇam muhur muhus
            <caesura/>
             tā<cb n="1"/>myamānaḥ sa kṛcchreṇa sannipātena mehate || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.8"> mūtravāhiṣu śalyena kṣateṣv abhihateṣu vā |
            <caesura/>
             srotaḥsu mūtrāghātas tu jāyate bhṛṣadāruṇaḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.9"> vātā<cb n="2"/>ghātena liṅgāni tasya tulyāni nirddiśet ||
            <caesura/>
             śakṛtas tu pratīghātād vāyur viguṇatāṃ gataḥ | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.10"> sādhmānañ ca samūla<lb n="4"/>ñ ca mūtrasaṅgaṃ karoti ca ||
            <caesura/>
             aśmarīsambhavasyoktaṃ mūtraghātasya lakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.11"> aśmarī śarkarā caiva śṛṇu kīrttaya<cb n="1"/><unclear
              reason="damage">to</unclear> mamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śarkarāyā viśeṣan tu śṛṇu kīrttayato mama | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.59.12"> pacyamānaṃ tu pittena śoṣyamānan tu vāyunā |

            a</unclear>bhisañjñitaṃ || </l>

              >ṃ</unclear> | yathoṣṇabhayāc chā<add place="bottom margin">yā</add>m anusarati || </l>

            kakṣe bhivṛddhiṃ gacchati tathā vātapittakaphaduṣṭo vraṇo bhivṛddhiṃ gacchatīti ||</l>

              pradhā<cb n="2"/>nā iti || </l>

            yavāgūr bhavatv i<lb n="5"/>ti || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.65.40"> yad anirdiṣṭaṃ buddhigamyan tad ūhyaṃ |
            <caesura/>

              >i</del> eva | ato dvitvam prasiddhim ity āha bhagavān dha<cb n="1"/>nvatariḥ | </l>
